####################################################################################################
STANDARD CAVE ENVIRONMENT FOUNDATION
####################################################################################################
Ultra-high-resolution, physically-based render of a NATURAL CAVE interior rich in geological majesty.  
Cathedral-scale granite & limestone architecture (#3C3C3C base, #8B4513 undertones) displays water-erosion striations, mineral veining, stalactites and smooth, time-worn floor paths (#4A4A4A).

STRUCTURAL SPECIFICATIONS
‚Ä¢ Walls   : Granite/limestone, layered veining, subtle mica sparkle (RMS roughness 0.55).  
‚Ä¢ Ceiling : Vaulted arches, stalactite chandeliers, skylight fissures.  
‚Ä¢ Floor   : Silky-eroded channels, pebble insets, centuries of foot smoothing.  

LIGHTING ARCHITECTURE
‚Ä¢ Key      : Filtered daylight shafts (6500 K ‚Üí 3200 K via rock bounce).  
‚Ä¢ Practical: Wall braziers & torches (#FFA500 / #FFD700) every 8 m for warm fill.  
‚Ä¢ Rim      : Soft red accent (H 10¬∞, S 80 %, V 90 %).  
‚Ä¢ Volumetrics: 8 % humidity haze, god-rays, dust motes 8 ‚Äì 25 ¬µm.

NATURAL ELEMENTS ¬∑ ATMOSPHERIC DETAILS
Underground stream (IOR 1.33), quartz clusters, stratified rock bands ¬∑ Mist fall-off 1.5 m, echo 0.25 s, ambient stone 16 ¬∞C.

SCALE & PROPORTION ¬∑ ZONE SPECIFICATIONS
Environment sized to elevate‚Äînot dwarf‚ÄîCapit√£o Caverna ¬∑ 1 Central Platform ¬∑ 2 Open Chambers ¬∑ 3 Wall Alcoves ¬∑ 4 Quiet Zones

TECHNICAL RENDERING
Resolution ‚â• 4096 px (still) / 4 K 16-bit EXR (video) ¬∑ Volumetric path-tracing ‚â• 256 spp, adaptive, denoise OFF.

CONTINUITY STANDARDS
Unified HDRI, seed-locked volumetrics, waterflow L‚ÜíR, dust ¬± 5 %.

CHARACTER‚ÄìENVIRONMENT INTEGRATION

STANDARD CAVE ENVIRONMENT FOUNDATION
####################################################################################################
Ultra-high-resolution, physically-based render of a NATURAL CAVE interior rich in geological majesty.  
Cathedral-scale granite & limestone architecture (#3C3C3C base, #8B4513 undertones) displays water-erosion striations, mineral veining, stalactites and smooth, time-worn floor paths (#4A4A4A).
STRUCTURAL SPECIFICATIONS
‚Ä¢ Walls   : Granite/limestone, layered veining, subtle mica sparkle (RMS roughness 0.55).  
‚Ä¢ Ceiling : Vaulted arches, stalactite chandeliers, skylight fissures.  
‚Ä¢ Floor   : Silky-eroded channels, pebble insets, centuries of foot smoothing.  
LIGHTING ARCHITECTURE
‚Ä¢ Key      : Filtered daylight shafts (6500 K ‚Üí 3200 K via rock bounce).  
‚Ä¢ Practical: Wall braziers & torches (#FFA500 / #FFD700) every 8 m for warm fill.  
‚Ä¢ Rim      : Soft red accent (H 10¬∞, S 80 %, V 90 %).  
‚Ä¢ Volumetrics: 8 % humidity haze, god-rays, dust motes 8 ‚Äì 25 ¬µm.
NATURAL ELEMENTS ¬∑ ATMOSPHERIC DETAILS
Underground stream (IOR 1.33), quartz clusters, stratified rock bands ¬∑ Mist fall-off 1.5 m, echo 0.25 s, ambient stone 16 ¬∞C.
SCALE & PROPORTION ¬∑ ZONE SPECIFICATIONS
Environment sized to elevate‚Äînot dwarf‚ÄîCapit√£o Caverna ¬∑ 1 Central Platform ¬∑ 2 Open Chambers ¬∑ 3 Wall Alcoves ¬∑ 4 Quiet Zones
TECHNICAL RENDERING
Resolution ‚â• 4096 px (still) / 4 K 16-bit EXR (video) ¬∑ Volumetric path-tracing ‚â• 256 spp, adaptive, denoise OFF.
CONTINUITY STANDARDS
Unified HDRI, seed-locked volumetrics, waterflow L‚ÜíR, dust ¬± 5 %.

‚Ä¢ Walls   : Granite/limestone, layered veining, subtle mica sparkle (RMS roughness 0.55).  
‚Ä¢ Ceiling : Vaulted arches, stalactite chandeliers, skylight fissures.  
‚Ä¢ Floor   : Silky-eroded channels, pebble insets, centuries of foot smoothing.  
LIGHTING ARCHITECTURE
‚Ä¢ Key      : Filtered daylight shafts (6500 K ‚Üí 3200 K via rock bounce).  
‚Ä¢ Practical: Wall braziers & torches (#FFA500 / #FFD700) every 8 m for warm fill.  
‚Ä¢ Rim      : Soft red accent (H 10¬∞, S 80 %, V 90 %).  
‚Ä¢ Volumetrics: 8 % humidity haze, god-rays, dust motes 8 ‚Äì 25 ¬µm.
NATURAL ELEMENTS ¬∑ ATMOSPHERIC DETAILS
Underground stream (IOR 1.33), quartz clusters, stratified rock bands ¬∑ Mist fall-off 1.5 m, echo 0.25 s, ambient stone 16 ¬∞C.
SCALE & PROPORTION ¬∑ ZONE SPECIFICATIONS
Environment sized to elevate‚Äînot dwarf‚ÄîCapit√£o Caverna ¬∑ 1 Central Platform ¬∑ 2 Open Chambers ¬∑ 3 Wall Alcoves ¬∑ 4 Quiet Zones
TECHNICAL RENDERING
Resolution ‚â• 4096 px (still) / 4 K 16-bit EXR (video) ¬∑ Volumetric path-tracing ‚â• 256 spp, adaptive, denoise OFF.
CONTINUITY STANDARDS
Unified HDRI, seed-locked volumetrics, waterflow L‚ÜíR, dust ¬± 5 %.

Ultra-high-resolution, physically-based render of a NATURAL CAVE interior rich in geological majesty.

‚Ä¢ Walls   : Granite/limestone, layered veining, subtle mica sparkle (RMS roughness 0.55).

‚Ä¢ Floor   : Silky-eroded channels, pebble insets, centuries of foot smoothing.

‚Ä¢ Key      : Filtered daylight shafts (6500 K ‚Üí 3200 K via rock bounce).

‚Ä¢ Rim      : Soft red accent (H 10¬∞, S 80 %, V 90 %).

Cathedral-scale granite & limestone architecture (#3C3C3C base, #8B4513 undertones) displays water-erosion striations, mineral veining, stalactites and smooth, time-worn floor paths (#4A4A4A).

‚Ä¢ Walls   : Granite/limestone, layered veining, subtle mica sparkle (RMS roughness 0.55).  
‚Ä¢ Ceiling : Vaulted arches, stalactite chandeliers, skylight fissures.  
‚Ä¢ Floor   : Silky-eroded channels, pebble insets, centuries of foot smoothing.

Pixar-style stylised wolf (grey top-coat, cream muzzle/ears, warm beige tail tip).  
Tall athletic hero ‚âà 6 heads; long legs = 50 % height; V-torso, narrow waist; digitigrade.  
Crimson eyes, thick brows; four dark-charcoal fingers.  
Wardrobe: fitted black hoodie + red ‚ñ≥ wolf logo (#FF3333, black draw-strings), black sweatpants, asymmetric black-and-white sneakers.
CHARACTER‚ÄìENVIRONMENT INTEGRATION
Warm torch fill + daylight key + red rim sculpt fur & musculature; physical floor shadow; subtle fire reflections on hoodie.
####################################################################################################
TEXTURE / RESOLUTION BOOST
####################################################################################################
Output 7680 √ó 4320 px 16-bit EXR (min 4096 √ó 2304) ¬∑ 8 K UDIM maps; anisotropic ON; displacement + micro-roughness; **NO** grain/bloom.
####################################################################################################
BRAND ACCURACY ‚Äî LOGO & COLORS
####################################################################################################
Equilateral ‚ñ≥ #FF3333 (45 % hoodie width) with centered howling-wolf cut-out; matte print roughness 0.8.
BRAND NEGATIVE PROMPT
(off-brand logo, wrong icon, gradient, faded print, low-res edge)

####################################################################################################
Overall height 6 heads ¬± 3 % ¬∑ Leg length 50 % ¬± 3 % (heel-to-hip) ¬∑ Knee at 25 % height ¬∑ Arm tips mid-thigh.
NEGATIVE PROPORTION PROMPT
(short legs, stubby, chubby stance, teddy build, bobble-head)
####################################################################################################
BODY SAFEGUARDS
####################################################################################################
Lean athletic | head ‚â§ 1.2√ó torso | digitigrade | NO plush/chibi/teddy | exactly 4 fingers | no mirrored shoes | no human-skin torso
####################################################################################################
HAND-COLOUR LOCK
####################################################################################################
‚Ä¢ Dorsal & side hand-fur  : cream-beige #C8A879  (identical to muzzle underside).  
‚Ä¢ Finger pads + claw tips : dark-charcoal #C8A879 (matte, no specular).  
‚Ä¢ No full-glove look, no dark mitten effect.  Preserve 3 fingers + thumb only.
HAND COLOUR NEGATIVE PROMPT
(dark gloves, black paws, soot-covered hand, full mitten, human skin tone, colour bleed)
####################################################################################################
FINGER-COUNT ENFORCEMENT
####################################################################################################
‚Ä¢ Hand anatomy : Exactly **4 digits per hand** (3 fingers + 1 thumb).  
‚Ä¢ Finger order : Thumb, index, middle, ring.  
‚Ä¢ No extra nubs, no vestigial pinky, no fused digits.  
FINGER NEGATIVE PROMPT
(five fingers, human hand, six fingers, extra digits, fused fingers, missing thumb)
####################################################################################################
NEGATIVE PROMPT (GLOBAL)
####################################################################################################
(cute, kawaii, plush, funko, chibi, mascot suit, fursuit, man in costume, wolf mask, toddler-proportions, five fingers, mirrored feet)
####################################################################################################
#######################  FRAME INSERT ‚Äî 11B: Crystal Reflection Moment ########################
EXACT LOCATION : Isolated alcove inside the cave, lined with glowing crystal veins and still water reflection basin.
CHARACTER POSITIONING : Capit√£o Caverna kneeling by a reflective crystal pool, one hand grazing the surface.
LIMB METRICS : Back straight, shoulder blades slightly pinched, tail low and still.
POSE SPECIFICS : Looking into reflection, palm extended flat over rippling water.
FACIAL EXPRESSION : Deep reflection; eyes narrow, soft tension in brow.
LIGHTING ON CHARACTER : Scroll light glow behind, crystal shimmer beneath. Facial shadows shaped by up-light.
CAMERA : Tight waist-up shot, low angle, focal point on eyes and pool.
ENVIRONMENTAL TOUCHES : Mirror image of character blurred by ripple; dim mist and warm flickers of cave torches in background.
VOICEOVER: "E agora‚Ä¶ s√≥ falta uma coisa: Explorar a Caverna!"

üé¨ FRAME 11C
####################################################################################################
STANDARD CAVE ENVIRONMENT FOUNDATION
####################################################################################################
Ultra-high-resolution, physically-based render of a NATURAL CAVE interior rich in geological majesty.  
Cathedral-scale granite & limestone architecture (#3C3C3C base, #8B4513 undertones) displays water-erosion striations, mineral veining, stalactites and smooth, time-worn floor paths (#4A4A4A).
STRUCTURAL SPECIFICATIONS
‚Ä¢ Walls   : Granite/limestone, layered veining, subtle mica sparkle (RMS roughness 0.55).  
‚Ä¢ Ceiling : Vaulted arches, stalactite chandeliers, skylight fissures.  
‚Ä¢ Floor   : Silky-eroded channels, pebble insets, centuries of foot smoothing.  
LIGHTING ARCHITECTURE
‚Ä¢ Key      : Filtered daylight shafts (6500 K ‚Üí 3200 K via rock bounce).  
‚Ä¢ Practical: Wall braziers & torches (#FFA500 / #FFD700) every 8 m for warm fill.  
‚Ä¢ Rim      : Soft red accent (H 10¬∞, S 80 %, V 90 %).  
‚Ä¢ Volumetrics: 8 % humidity haze, god-rays, dust motes 8 ‚Äì 25 ¬µm.
NATURAL ELEMENTS ¬∑ ATMOSPHERIC DETAILS
Underground stream (IOR 1.33), quartz clusters, stratified rock bands ¬∑ Mist fall-off 1.5 m, echo 0.25 s, ambient stone 16 ¬∞C.
SCALE & PROPORTION ¬∑ ZONE SPECIFICATIONS
Environment sized to elevate‚Äînot dwarf‚ÄîCapit√£o Caverna ¬∑ 1 Central Platform ¬∑ 2 Open Chambers ¬∑ 3 Wall Alcoves ¬∑ 4 Quiet Zones
TECHNICAL RENDERING
Resolution ‚â• 4096 px (still) / 4 K 16-bit EXR (video) ¬∑ Volumetric path-tracing ‚â• 256 spp, adaptive, denoise OFF.
CONTINUITY STANDARDS
Unified HDRI, seed-locked volumetrics, waterflow L‚ÜíR, dust ¬± 5 %.
